role="img"><title>Anthropic</title><path d="M17.3041 3.541h-3.6718l6.696 16.918H24Zm-10.6082 0L0 20.459h3.7442l1.3693-3.5527h7.0052l1.3693 3.5528h3.7442L10.5363 3.5409Zm-.3712 10.2232 2.2914-5.9456 class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useAsyncList</code> hook manages asynchronous data operations for list collections. It provides a comprehensive solution
for loading, filtering, sorting, and paginating data with built-in loading states, error handling, and request
cancellation.</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">import</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> { useAsyncList } </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">from</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> &#x27;@ark-ui/react/collection&#x27;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> list</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF"> useAsyncList</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;</span><span style="color:#FFA657">User</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">  async</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF"> load</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">({ </span><span style="color:#FFA657">signal</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> }) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">    const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> response</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> await</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF"> fetch</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;/api/users&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, { signal })</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">    const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> users</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> await</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> response.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">json</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">()</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">    return</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> { items: users }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">})</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">console.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">log</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(list.items) </span><span style="color:#8B949E">// User[]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">console.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">log</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(list.loading) </span><span style="color:#8B949E">// boolean</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">console.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">log</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(list.error) </span><span style="color:#8B949E">// Error | null</span></span></code></pre>
<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<h3 id="loading-data" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#loading-data"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Loading Data</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Load data asynchronously from an API using the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">load</code> function and update the list when the data is ready.</p>

<h3 id="sorting-server-side" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#sorting-server-side"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Sorting (Server-side)</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Send sort parameters to the server and reload data when sorting changes.</p>

<h3 id="dependencies" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#dependencies"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Dependencies</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Automatically reload data when dependencies change, such as filter selections or external state.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_99hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_99hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_99hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>
<h3 id="props" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#props"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Props</h3>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">load</strong> (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">(params: LoadParams&lt;C&gt;) =&gt; Promise&lt;LoadResult&lt;T, C&gt;&gt;</code>) - Function to load data asynchronously</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">sort</strong> (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">(params: SortParams&lt;T&gt;) =&gt; Promise&lt;SortResult&lt;T&gt;&gt; | SortResult&lt;T&gt;</code>) - Optional function for client-side
sorting</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">autoReload</strong> (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">boolean</code>, default: <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">false</code>) - Whether to automatically reload data on mount</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">initialItems</strong> (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">T[]</code>, default: <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">[]</code>) - Initial items to display before first load</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">dependencies</strong> (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">any[]</code>, default: <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">[]</code>) - Values that trigger a reload when changed</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">initialFilterText</strong> (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">string</code>, default: <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">&#x27;&#x27;</code>) - Initial filter text value</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">initialSortDescriptor</strong> (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">SortDescriptor | null</code>) - Initial sort configuration</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="load-parameters" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#load-parameters"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Load Parameters</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">load</code> function receives an object with the following properties:</p>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">cursor</strong> (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">C | undefined</code>) - Current cursor for pagination</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">filterText</strong> (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">string</code>) - Current filter text</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">sortDescriptor</strong> (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">SortDescriptor | null</code>) - Current sort configuration</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">signal</strong> (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">AbortSignal</code>) - AbortController signal for request cancellation</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="load-result" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#load-result"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Load Result</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">load</code> function should return an object with:</p>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">items</strong> (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">T[]</code>) - The loaded items</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">cursor</strong> (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">C | undefined</code>) - Optional cursor for next page</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="sort-parameters" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#sort-parameters"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Sort Parameters</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">sort</code> function receives an object with:</p>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">items</strong> (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">T[]</code>) - Current items to sort</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">descriptor</strong> (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">SortDescriptor</code>) - Sort configuration with <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">column</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">direction</code></li>
</ul>
<h3 id="return-value" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#return-value"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Return Value</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The hook returns an object with the following properties and methods:</p>
<h4 id="state-properties" class="mt_1.5em mb_0.5em lh_1.5 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#state-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>State Properties</h4>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">items</strong> (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">T[]</code>) - Current list of items</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">loading</strong> (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">boolean</code>) - Whether a load operation is in progress</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">error</strong> (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Error | null</code>) - Any error from the last operation</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">cursor</strong> (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">C | undefined</code>) - Current cursor for pagination</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">filterText</strong> (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">string</code>) - Current filter text</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">sortDescriptor</strong> (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">SortDescriptor | null</code>) - Current sort configuration</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="methods" class="mt_1.5em mb_0.5em lh_1.5 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#methods"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Methods</h4>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">reload</strong> (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">() =&gt; void</code>) - Reload data from the beginning</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">loadMore</strong> (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">() =&gt; void</code>) - Load more items (when cursor is available)</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">setFilterText</strong> (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">(text: string) =&gt; void</code>) - Set filter text and reload</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">sort</strong> (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">(descriptor: SortDescriptor) =&gt; void</code>) - Apply sorting</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="types" class="mt_1.5em mb_0.5em lh_1.5 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#types"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Types</h4>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">interface</span><span style="color:#FFA657"> LoadParams</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;</span><span style="color:#FFA657">C</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt; {</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">interface</span><span style="color:#FFA657"> LoadResult</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;</span><span style="color:#FFA657">T</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, </span><span style="color:#FFA657">C</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt; {</span></span>

`useAsyncList` hook manages asynchronous data operations for list collections. It provides a comprehensive solution\nfor loading, filtering, sorting, and paginating data with built-in loading states, error handling, and request\ncancellation.\n\n```tsx\nimport { useAsyncList } from '@ark-ui/react/collection'\n\nconst list = useAsyncList\u003cUser\u003e({\n  async load({ signal }) {\n    const response = await fetch('/api/users', { signal })\n    const users = await response.json()\n    return { items: users }\n  },\n})\n\nconsole.log(list.items) // User[]\nconsole.log(list.loading) // boolean\nconsole.log(list.error) // Error | null\n```\n\n## Examples\n\n### Loading Data\n\nLoad data asynchronously from an API using the `load` function and update the list when the data is ready.\n\n**Example: async-list/reload**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { useAsyncList } from '@ark-ui/react/collection'\nimport { LoaderIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/async-list.module.css'\n\ninterface Quote {\n  id: number\n  quote: string\n  author: string\n}\n\nexport const Reload = () =\u003e {\n  const list = useAsyncList\u003cQuote\u003e({\n    autoReload: true,\n    async load() {\n      const response = await fetch(`https://dummyjson.com/quotes?limit=4\u0026skip=${Math.floor(Math.random() * 50)}`)\n\n      if (!response.ok) {\n        throw new Error('Failed to fetch quotes')\n      }\n\n      const data = await response.json()\n      return { items: data.quotes }\n    },\n  })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv className={styles.Header}\u003e\n        \u003cbutton className={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e list.reload()} disabled={list.loading}\u003e\n          {list.loading ? (\n            \u003c\u003e\n              \u003cLoaderIcon className={styles.Spinner} /\u003e Loading\n            \u003c/\u003e\n          ) : (\n            'Reload Quotes'\n          )}\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      {list.error \u0026\u0026 \u003cdiv className={styles.Error}\u003eError: {list.error.message}\u003c/div\u003e}\n\n      \u003cdiv className={styles.ItemGroup}\u003e\n        {list.items.map((quote) =\u003e (\n          \u003cdiv key={quote.id} className={styles.Item}\u003e\n            \u003cdiv className={styles.ItemContent}\u003e\n              \u003cdiv className={styles.ItemDescription}\u003e\"{quote.quote}\"\u003c/div\u003e\n              \u003cdiv className={styles.ItemMeta}\u003e— {quote.author}\u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/div\u003e\n        ))}\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { useAsyncList } from '@ark-ui/solid/collection'\nimport { LoaderIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { For } from 'solid-js'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/async-list.module.css'\n\ninterface Quote {\n  id: number\n  quote: string\n  author: string\n}\n\nexport const Reload = () =\u003e {\n  const list = useAsyncList\u003cQuote\u003e({\n    autoReload: true,\n    async load() {\n      const response = await fetch(`https://dummyjson.com/quotes?limit=4\u0026skip=${Math.floor(Math.random() * 50)}`)\n\n      if (!response.ok) {\n        throw new Error('Failed to fetch quotes')\n      }\n\n      const data = await response.json()\n      return { items: data.quotes }\n    },\n  })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv class={styles.Header}\u003e\n        \u003cbutton class={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e list().reload()} disabled={list().loading}\u003e\n          {list().loading ? (\n            \u003c\u003e\n              \u003cLoaderIcon class={styles.Spinner} /\u003e Loading\n            \u003c/\u003e\n          ) : (\n            'Reload Quotes'\n          )}\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      {list().error \u0026\u0026 \u003cdiv class={styles.Error}\u003eError: {list().error.message}\u003c/div\u003e}\n\n      \u003cdiv class={styles.ItemGroup}\u003e\n        \u003cFor each={list().items}\u003e\n          {(quote) =\u003e (\n            \u003cdiv class={styles.Item}\u003e\n              \u003cdiv class={styles.ItemContent}\u003e\n                \u003cdiv class={styles.ItemDescription}\u003e\"{quote.quote}\"\u003c/div\u003e\n                \u003cdiv class={styles.ItemMeta}\u003e— {quote.author}\u003c/div\u003e\n              \u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/For\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  autoReload: true,\n  async load() {\n    const response = await fetch(`https://dummyjson.com/quotes?limit=4\u0026skip=${Math.floor(Math.random() * 50)}`)\n\n    if (!response.ok) {\n      throw new Error('Failed to fetch quotes')\n    }\n\n    const data = await response.json()\n    return { items: data.quotes }\n  },\n})\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv async-list/infinite-loading**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { useAsyncList } from '@ark-ui/react/collection'\nimport { LoaderIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/async-list.module.css'\n\nconst LIMIT = 4\n\ninterface Post {\n  userId: number\n  id: number\n  title: string\n  body: string\n}\n\nexport const InfiniteLoading = () =\u003e {\n  const list = useAsyncList\u003cPost, number\u003e({\n    autoReload: true,\n    async load({ cursor }) {\n      const page = cursor || 1\n      const start = (page - 1) * LIMIT\n\n      const response = await fetch(`https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/posts?_start=${start}\u0026_limit=${LIMIT}`)\n\n      if (!response.ok) {\n        throw new Error('Failed to fetch posts')\n      }\n\n      const posts: Post[] = await response.json()\n      const hasNextPage = posts.length === LIMIT\n\n      return {\n        items: posts,\n        cursor: hasNextPage ? page + 1 : undefined,\n      }\n    },\n  })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv className={styles.Header}\u003e\n        \u003cspan className={styles.Status}\u003e\n          Loaded {list.items.length} posts\n          {list.cursor \u0026\u0026 ` (more available)`}\n        \u003c/span\u003e\n        {list.cursor \u0026\u0026 (\n          \u003cbutton className={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e list.loadMore()} disabled={list.loading}\u003e\n            {list.loading ? (\n              \u003c\u003e\n                \u003cLoaderIcon className={styles.Spinner} /\u003e Loading\n              \u003c/\u003e\n            ) : (\n              'Load More'\n            )}\n          \u003c/button\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      {list.error \u0026\u0026 \u003cdiv className={styles.Error}\u003eError: {list.error.message}\u003c/div\u003e}\n\n      \u003cdiv className={styles.ItemGroup}\u003e\n        {list.items.map((post, index) =\u003e (\n          \u003cdiv key={post.id} className={styles.Item}\u003e\n            \u003cdiv className={styles.ItemContent}\u003e\n              \u003cdiv className={styles.ItemTitle}\u003e\n                {index + 1}. {post.title}\n              \u003c/div\u003e\n              \u003cdiv className={styles.ItemDescription}\u003e{post.body}\u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/div\u003e\n        ))}\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { useAsyncList } from '@ark-ui/solid/collection'\nimport { LoaderIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { For } from 'solid-js'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/async-list.module.css'\n\nconst LIMIT = 4\n\ninterface Post {\n  userId: number\n  id: number\n  title: string\n  body: string\n}\n\nexport const InfiniteLoading = () =\u003e {\n  const list = useAsyncList\u003cPost, number\u003e({\n    autoReload: true,\n    async load({ cursor }) {\n      const page = cursor || 1\n      const start = (page - 1) * LIMIT\n\n      const response = await fetch(`https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/posts?_start=${start}\u0026_limit=${LIMIT}`)\n\n      if (!response.ok) {\n        throw new Error('Failed to fetch posts')\n      }\n\n      const posts: Post[] = await response.json()\n      const hasNextPage = posts.length === LIMIT\n\n      return {\n        items: posts,\n        cursor: hasNextPage ? page + 1 : undefined,\n      }\n    },\n  })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv class={styles.Header}\u003e\n        \u003cspan class={styles.Status}\u003e\n          Loaded {list().items.length} posts\n          {list().cursor \u0026\u0026 ` (more available)`}\n        \u003c/span\u003e\n        {list().cursor \u0026\u0026 (\n          \u003cbutton class={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e list().loadMore()} disabled={list().loading}\u003e\n            {list().loading ? (\n              \u003c\u003e\n                \u003cLoaderIcon class={styles.Spinner} /\u003e Loading\n              \u003c/\u003e\n            ) : (\n              'Load More'\n            )}\n          \u003c/button\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      {list().error \u0026\u0026 \u003cdiv class={styles.Error}\u003eError: {list().error.message}\u003c/div\u003e}\n\n      \u003cdiv class={styles.ItemDescription}\u003e{post.body}\u003c/div\u003e\n              \u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/For\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { useAsyncList } from '@ark-ui/vue/collection'\nimport { LoaderIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/async-list.module.css'\n\nconst LIMIT = 5\n\ninterface Post {\n  userId: number\n  id: number\n  title: string\n  body: string\n}\n\nconst list = useAsyncList\u003cPost, number\u003e({\n  autoReload: true,\n  async load({ cursor }) {\n    const page = cursor || 1\n    const start = (page - 1) * LIMIT\n\n    const response = await fetch(`https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/posts?_start=${start}\u0026_limit=${LIMIT}`)\n\n    if (!response.ok) {\n      throw new Error('Failed to fetch posts')\n    }\n\n    const posts: Post[] = await response.json()\n    const hasNextPage = posts.length === LIMIT\n\n    return {\n      items: posts,\n      cursor: hasNextPage ? page + 1 : undefined,\n    }\n  },\n})\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n    \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.Header\"\u003e\n      \u003cbutton v-if=\"list.cursor\" :class=\"button.Root\" @click=\"list.loadMore()\" :disabled=\"list.loading\"\u003e\n        \u003ctemplate v-if=\"list.loading\"\u003e\n          \u003cLoaderIcon :class=\"styles.Spinner\" /\u003e\n          Loading\n        \u003c/template\u003e\n        \u003ctemplate v-else\u003eLoad More\u003c/template\u003e\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n\n    \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.Status\"\u003e\n      Loaded {{ list.items.length }} posts\n      \u003cspan v-if=\"list.cursor\"\u003e(more available)\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n\n    \u003cdiv v-if=\"list.error\" :class=\"styles.Error\"\u003eError: {{ list.error.message }}\u003c/div\u003e\n\n    \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.ItemGroup\"\u003e\n      \u003cdiv v-for=\"(post, index) in list.items\" :key=\"post.id\" :class=\"styles.Item\"\u003e\n        \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.ItemContent\"\u003e\n          \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.ItemTitle\"\u003e{{ index + 1 }}. {{ post.title }}\u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.ItemDescription\"\u003e{{ post.body }}\u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { useAsyncList } from '@ark-ui/svelte/collection'\n  import { LoaderIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/async-list.module.css'\n\n  const LIMIT = 4\n\n  interface Post {\n    userId: number\n    id: number\n    title: string\n    body: string\n  }\n\n  const list = useAsyncList\u003cPost, number\u003e({\n    autoReload: true,\n    async load({ cursor }) {\n      const page = cursor || 1\n      const start = (page - 1) * LIMIT\n\n      const response = await fetch(`https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/posts?_start=${start}\u0026_limit=${LIMIT}`)\n\n      if (!response.ok) {\n        throw new Error('Failed to fetch posts')\n      }\n\n      const posts: Post[] = await response.json()\n      const hasNextPage = posts.length === LIMIT\n\n      return {\n        items: posts,\n        cursor: hasNextPage ? page + 1 : undefined,\n      }\n    },\n  })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class={styles.Root}\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class={styles.Header}\u003e\n    \u003cspan class={styles.Status}\u003e\n      Loaded {list().items.length} posts\n      {#if list().cursor}(more available){/if}\n    \u003c/span\u003e\n    {#if list().cursor}\n      \u003cbutton class={button.Root} onclick={() =\u003e list().loadMore()} disabled={list().loading}\u003e\n        {#if list().loading}\n          \u003cLoaderIcon class={styles.Spinner} /\u003e Loading\n        {:else}\n          Load More\n        {/if}\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n    {/if}\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\n  {#if list().error}\n    \u003cdiv class={styles.Error}\u003eError: {list().error.message}\u003c/div\u003e\n  {/if}\n\n  \u003cdiv class={styles.ItemGroup}\u003e\n    {#each list().items as post, index}\n      \u003cdiv class={styles.Item}\u003e\n        \u003cdiv class={styles.ItemContent}\u003e\n          \u003cdiv class={styles.ItemTitle}\u003e{index + 1}. {post.title}\u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003cdiv class={styles.ItemDescription}\u003e{post.body}\u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    {/each}\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Filtering\n\nFilter data based on user input with automatic debouncing and loading states.\n\n**Example: async-list/filter**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { useAsyncList } from '@ark-ui/react/collection'\nimport { LoaderIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/async-list.module.css'\n\nconst LIMIT = 4\n\ninterface User {\n  id: number\n  name: string\n  email: string\n  department: string\n  role: string\n}\n\nexport const Filter = () =\u003e {\n  const list = useAsyncList\u003cUser\u003e({\n    initialItems: mockUsers.slice(0, LIMIT),\n    async load({ filterText }) {\n      await delay(500)\n\n      if (!filterText) {\n        return { items: mockUsers.slice(0, LIMIT) }\n      }\n\n      const filtered = mockUsers.filter(\n        (user) =\u003e\n          user.name.toLowerCase().includes(filterText.toLowerCase()) ||\n          user.email.toLowerCase().includes(filterText.toLowerCase()),\n      )\n\n      return { items: filtered.slice(0, LIMIT) }\n    },\n  })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv className={styles.Header}\u003e\n        \u003cinput\n          className={field.Input}\n          type=\"text\"\n          placeholder=\"Search users...\"\n          value={list.filterText}\n          onChange={(e) =\u003e list.setFilterText(e.target.value)}\n        /\u003e\n        {list.loading \u0026\u0026 (\n          \u003cspan className={styles.Loading}\u003e\n            \u003cLoaderIcon className={styles.Spinner} /\u003e Searching\n          \u003c/span\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      {list.error \u0026\u0026 \u003cdiv className={styles.Error}\u003eError: {list.error.message}\u003c/div\u003e}\n\n      \u003cdiv className={styles.ItemGroup}\u003e\n        {list.items.map((user) =\u003e (\n          \u003cdiv key={user.id} className={styles.Item}\u003e\n            \u003cdiv className={styles.ItemContent}\u003e\n              \u003cdiv className={styles.ItemTitle}\u003e{user.name}\u003c/div\u003e\n              \u003cdiv className={styles.ItemDescription}\u003e{user.email}\u003c/div\u003e\n              \u003cdiv className={styles.ItemMeta}\u003e\n                {user.department} • {user.role}\n              \u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/div\u003e\n        ))}\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      {list.items.length === 0 \u0026\u0026 !list.loading \u0026\u0026 \u003cdiv className={styles.Empty}\u003eNo results found\u003c/div\u003e}\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\nconst delay = (ms: number) =\u003e new Promise((resolve) =\u003e setTimeout(resolve, ms))\n\nconst mockUsers: User[] = [\n  { id: 1, name: 'Alice Johnson', email: 'alice@example.com', department: 'Engineering', role: 'Senior Developer' },\n  { id: 2, name: 'Bob Smith', email: 'bob@example.com', user.name.toLowerCase().includes(filterText.toLowerCase()) ||\n          user.email.toLowerCase().includes(filterText.toLowerCase()),\n      )\n\n      return { items: filtered.slice(0, LIMIT) }\n    },\n  })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class={styles.Root}\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class={styles.Header}\u003e\n    \u003cinput\n      class={field.Input}\n      type=\"text\"\n      placeholder=\"Search users...\"\n      value={list().filterText}\n      oninput={(e) =\u003e list().setFilterText(e.currentTarget.value)}\n    /\u003e\n    {#if list().loading}\n      \u003cspan class={styles.Loading}\u003e\n        \u003cLoaderIcon class={styles.Spinner} /\u003e Searching\n      \u003c/span\u003e\n    {/if}\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\n  {#if list().error}\n    \u003cdiv class={styles.Error}\u003eError: {list().error.message}\u003c/div\u003e\n  {/if}\n\n  \u003cdiv class={styles.ItemGroup}\u003e\n    {#each list().items as user}\n      \u003cdiv class={styles.Item}\u003e\n        \u003cdiv class={styles.ItemContent}\u003e\n          \u003cdiv class={styles.ItemTitle}\u003e{user.name}\u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003cdiv class={styles.ItemDescription}\u003e{user.email}\u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003cdiv class={styles.ItemMeta}\u003e\n            {user.department} • {user.role}\n          \u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    {/each}\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\n  {#if list().items.length === 0 \u0026\u0026 !list().loading}\n    \u003cdiv class={styles.Empty}\u003eNo results found\u003c/div\u003e\n  {/if}\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Sorting (Client-side)\n\nSort data on the client side after loading from the server.\n\n**Example: async-list/sort-client-side**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { useAsyncList } from '@ark-ui/react/collection'\nimport { useCollator } from '@ark-ui/react/locale'\nimport { ArrowDownIcon, ArrowUpDownIcon, ArrowUpIcon, LoaderIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/async-list.module.css'\n\ninterface User {\n  id: number\n  name: string\n  username: string\n  email: string\n  phone: string\n  website: string\n}\n\nexport const SortClientSide = () =\u003e {\n  const collator = useCollator()\n\n  const list = useAsyncList\u003cUser\u003e({\n    autoReload: true,\n    load: async () =\u003e {\n      const response = await fetch('https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/users?_limit=5')\n      const data = await response.json()\n      return { items: data }\n    },\n    sort({ items, descriptor }) {\n      return {\n        items: items.sort((a, b) =\u003e {\n          const { column, direction } = descriptor\n          let cmp = collator.compare(String(a[column]), String(b[column]))\n          if (direction === 'descending') {\n            cmp *= -1\n          }\n          return cmp\n        }),\n      }\n    },\n  })\n\n  const handleSort = (column: keyof User) =\u003e {\n    const currentSort = list.sortDescriptor\n    let direction: 'ascending' | 'descending' = 'ascending'\n\n    if (currentSort?.column === column \u0026\u0026 currentSort.direction === 'ascending') {\n      direction = 'descending'\n    }\n\n    list.sort({ column, direction })\n  }\n\n  const getSortIcon = (column: keyof User) =\u003e {\n    const current = list.sortDescriptor\n    if (current?.column !== column) return \u003cArrowUpDownIcon /\u003e\n    return current.direction === 'ascending' ? \u003cArrowUpIcon /\u003e : \u003cArrowDownIcon /\u003e\n  }\n\n  const descriptor = list.sortDescriptor\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className={styles.Root}\u003e\n      {list.loading \u0026\u0026 (\n        \u003cdiv className={styles.Loading}\u003e\n          \u003cLoaderIcon className={styles.Spinner} /\u003e Loading\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n      )}\n      {list.error \u0026\u0026 \u003cdiv className={styles.Error}\u003eError: {list.error.message}\u003c/div\u003e}\n      \u003cdiv className={styles.Status}\u003e\n        Sorted by: {descriptor ? `${descriptor.column} (${descriptor.direction})` : 'none'}\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      \u003ctable className={styles.Table}\u003e\n        \u003cthead\u003e\n          \u003ctr\u003e\n            {[\n              { key: 'name', label: 'Name' },\n              { key: 'username', label: 'Username' },\n              { key: 'email', label: 'Email' },\n            ].map(({ key, label }) =\u003e (\n              \u003cth key={key} onClick={() =\u003e handleSort(key as keyof User)}\u003e\n                {label} {getSortIcon(key as keyof User)}\n              \u003c/th\u003e\n            ))}\n          \u003c/tr\u003e\n        \u003c/thead\u003e\n        \u003ctbody\u003e\n          {list.items.map((user) =\u003e (\n            \u003ctr key={user.id}\u003e\n              \u003ctd\u003e{user.name}\u003c/td\u003e\n              \u003ctd\u003e{user.username}\u003c/td\u003e\n              \u003ctd\u003e{user.email}\u003c/td\u003e\n            \u003c/tr\u003e\n          ))}\n        \u003c/tbody\u003e\n      \u003c/table\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { useAsyncList } from '@ark-ui/solid/collection'\nimport { useCollator } from '@ark-ui/solid/locale'\nimport { ArrowDownIcon, ArrowUpDownIcon, ArrowUpIcon, LoaderIcon } from \u003ctd\u003e{user.username}\u003c/td\u003e\n                \u003ctd\u003e{user.email}\u003c/td\u003e\n              \u003c/tr\u003e\n            )}\n          \u003c/For\u003e\n        \u003c/tbody\u003e\n      \u003c/table\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { useAsyncList } from '@ark-ui/vue/collection'\nimport { useCollator } from '@ark-ui/vue/locale'\nimport { ArrowDownIcon, ArrowUpDownIcon, ArrowUpIcon, LoaderIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { computed } from 'vue'\nimport styles from 'styles/async-list.module.css'\n\ninterface User {\n  id: number\n  name: string\n  username: string\n  email: string\n  phone: string\n  website: string\n}\n\nconst collator = useCollator()\n\nconst list = useAsyncList\u003cUser\u003e({\n  autoReload: true,\n  load: async () =\u003e {\n    const response = await fetch('https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/users?_limit=5')\n    const data = await response.json()\n    return { items: data }\n  },\n  sort({ items, descriptor }) {\n    return {\n      items: items.sort((a, b) =\u003e {\n        const { column, direction } = descriptor\n        let cmp = collator.value.compare(String(a[column]), String(b[column]))\n        if (direction === 'descending') {\n          cmp *= -1\n        }\n        return cmp\n      }),\n    }\n  },\n})\n\nconst columns = [\n  { key: 'name', label: 'Name' },\n  { key: 'username', label: 'Username' },\n  { key: 'email', label: 'Email' },\n]\n\nconst handleSort = (column: keyof User) =\u003e {\n  const currentSort = list.value.sortDescriptor\n  let direction: 'ascending' | 'descending' = 'ascending'\n\n  if (currentSort?.column === column \u0026\u0026 currentSort.direction === 'ascending') {\n    direction = 'descending'\n  }\n\n  list.value.sort({ column, direction })\n}\n\nconst descriptor = interface User {\n    id: number\n    name: string\n    username: string\n    email: string\n    phone: string\n    website: string\n  }\n\n  const collator = useCollator()\n\n  const list = response.json()\n      return { items: data }\n    },\n    sort({ items, descriptor }) {\n      return {\n        items: items.sort((a, b) =\u003e {\n          const { column, direction } = descriptor\n          let cmp = collator().compare(String(a[column]), String(b[column]))\n          if (direction === 'descending') {\n            cmp *= -1\n          }\n          return cmp\n \u003c/table\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Sorting (Server-side)\n\nSend sort parameters to the server and reload data when sorting changes.\n\n**Example: async-list/sort-server-side**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { useAsyncList } from '@ark-ui/react/collection'\nimport { ArrowDownIcon, ArrowUpDownIcon, ArrowUpIcon, LoaderIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/async-list.module.css'\n\ninterface Product {\n  id: number\n  title: string\n  price: number\n  description: string\n  category: string\n  image: string\n  rating: {\n    rate: number\n    count: number\n  }\n}\n\nexport const SortServerSide = () =\u003e {\n  const list = useAsyncList\u003cProduct\u003e({\n    autoReload: true,\n    async load({ sortDescriptor }) {\n      const url = new URL('https://fakestoreapi.com/products')\n      url.searchParams.set('limit', '5')\n      if (sortDescriptor) {\n        const { direction } = sortDescriptor\n        url.searchParams.set('sort', direction === 'ascending' ? 'asc' : 'desc')\n      }\n      const response = await fetch(url)\n      const items = await response.json()\n      return { items }\n    },\n  })\n\n  const handleSort = (column: keyof Product) =\u003e {\n    const currentSort = list.sortDescriptor\n    let direction: 'ascending' | 'descending' = 'ascending'\n    if (currentSort?.column === column \u0026\u0026 currentSort.direction === 'ascending') {\n      direction = 'descending'\n    }\n    list.sort({ column, direction })\n  }\n\n  const getSortIcon = (column: keyof Product) =\u003e {\n    const desc = list.sortDescriptor\n    if (desc?.column !== column) return \u003cArrowUpDownIcon /\u003e\n    return desc.direction === 'ascending' ? \u003cArrowUpIcon /\u003e : \u003cArrowDownIcon /\u003e\n  }\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv className={styles.Header}\u003e\n        \u003cbutton className={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e handleSort('title')}\u003e\n          Sort by title {getSortIcon('title')}\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        {list.loading \u0026\u0026 (\n          \u003cspan className={styles.Loading}\u003e\n            \u003cLoaderIcon className={styles.Spinner} /\u003e Loading\n          \u003c/span\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      {list.error \u0026\u0026 \u003cdiv className={styles.Error}\u003eError: {list.error.message}\u003c/div\u003e}\n\n      \u003cdiv className={styles.ItemGroup}\u003e\n        {list.items.map((product) =\u003e (\n          \u003cdiv key={product.id} className={styles.Item} data-variant=\"outline\"\u003e\n            \u003cdiv className={styles.ItemMedia}\u003e\n              \u003cimg src={product.image} alt={product.title} /\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003cdiv className={styles.ItemContent}\u003e\n              \u003cdiv className={styles.ItemTitle}\u003e{product.title}\u003c/div\u003e\n              \u003cdiv className={styles.ItemDescription}\u003e${product.price}\u003c/div\u003e\n              \u003cdiv className={styles.ItemMeta}\u003e\n                {product.category} • {product.rating.rate} ({product.rating.count} reviews)\n              \u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/div\u003e\n        ))}\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { useAsyncList } from '@ark-ui/solid/collection'\nimport { ArrowDownIcon, ArrowUpDownIcon, ArrowUpIcon, LoaderIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { For } ({product.rating.count} reviews)\n                \u003c/div\u003e\n              \u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/For\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { useAsyncList } from '@ark-ui/vue/collection'\nimport { ArrowDownIcon, ArrowUpDownIcon, ArrowUpIcon, LoaderIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/async-list.module.css'\n\ninterface Product {\n  id: number\n  title: string\n  price: number\n  description: string\n  category: string\n  image: string\n  rating: {\n    rate: number\n    count: number\n  }\n}\n\nconst list = useAsyncList\u003cProduct\u003e({\n  autoReload: true,\n  async load({ sortDescriptor }) {\n    const url = new URL('https://fakestoreapi.com/products')\n    url.searchParams.set('limit', '5')\n    if (sortDescriptor) {\n      const { direction } = sortDescriptor\n      url.searchParams.set('sort', direction === 'ascending' ? 'asc' : 'desc')\n    }\n    const response = await fetch(url)\n    const items = await response.json()\n    return { items }\n  },\n})\n\nconst handleSort = (column: keyof Product) =\u003e {\n  const currentSort = list.value.sortDescriptor\n  let direction: 'ascending' | 'descending' = 'ascending'\n  if (currentSort?.column === column \u0026\u0026 currentSort.direction === 'ascending') {\n    direction = 'descending'\n  }\n  list.value.sort({ column, direction })\n}\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n    \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.Header\"\u003e\n      \u003cbutton :class=\"button.Root\" @click=\"handleSort('title')\"\u003e\n        Sort by title\n        \u003ctemplate v-if=\"list.sortDescriptor?.column === 'title'\"\u003e\n          \u003cArrowUpIcon v-if=\"list.sortDescriptor?.direction === 'ascending'\" /\u003e\n          \u003cArrowDownIcon v-else /\u003e\n        \u003c/template\u003e\n        \u003cArrowUpDownIcon v-else /\u003e\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003cspan v-if=\"list.loading\" :class=\"styles.Loading\"\u003e\n        \u003cLoaderIcon :class=\"styles.Spinner\" /\u003e\n        Loading\n      \u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n\n    \u003cdiv v-if=\"list.error\" :class=\"styles.Error\"\u003eError: {{ list.error.message }}\u003c/div\u003e\n\n    \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.ItemGroup\"\u003e\n      \u003cdiv v-for=\"product in list.items\" :key=\"product.id\" :class=\"styles.Item\" data-variant=\"outline\"\u003e\n        \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.ItemMedia\"\u003e\n          \u003cimg :src=\"product.image\" :alt=\"product.title\" /\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.ItemContent\"\u003e\n          \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.ItemTitle\"\u003e{{ product.title }}\u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.ItemDescription\"\u003e${{ product.price }}\u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.ItemMeta\"\u003e\n            {{ product.category }} • {{ product.rating.rate }} ({{ product.rating.count }} reviews)\n          \u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { useAsyncList } from '@ark-ui/svelte/collection'\n  import { ArrowDownIcon, ArrowUpDownIcon, ArrowUpIcon, LoaderIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/async-list.module.css'\n\n  interface Product {\n    id: number\n    title: string\n    price: number\n    description: string\n    category: string\n    image: string\n    rating: {\n      rate: number\n      count: number\n    }\n  }\n\n  const list = useAsyncList\u003cProduct\u003e({\n    autoReload: true,\n    async load({ sortDescriptor }) {\n      const url = new URL('https://fakestoreapi.com/products')\n      url.searchParams.set('limit', '5')\n      if (sortDescriptor) {\n        const { direction } = sortDescriptor\n        url.searchParams.set('sort', direction === 'ascending' ? 'asc' : 'desc')\n      }\n      const response = await fetch(url)\n      const items = await response.json()\n      return { items }\n    },\n  })\n\n  const handleSort = (column: keyof Product) =\u003e {\n    const currentSort = list().sortDescriptor\n    let direction: 'ascending' | 'descending' = 'ascending'\n    if (currentSort?.column === column \u0026\u0026 currentSort.direction === 'ascending') {\n      direction = 'descending'\n    }\n    list().sort({ column, direction })\n  }\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class={styles.Root}\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class={styles.Header}\u003e\n    \u003cbutton class={button.Root} onclick={() =\u003e handleSort('title')}\u003e\n      Sort by title\n      {#if list().sortDescriptor?.column === 'title'}\n        {#if list().sortDescriptor?.direction === 'ascending'}\n          \u003cArrowUpIcon /\u003e\n        {:else}\n          \u003cArrowDownIcon /\u003e\n        {/if}\n      {:else}\n        \u003cArrowUpDownIcon /\u003e\n      {/if}\n    \u003c/button\u003e\n    {#if list().loading}\n      \u003cspan class={styles.Loading}\u003e\n        \u003cLoaderIcon class={styles.Spinner} /\u003e class={styles.ItemGroup}\u003e\n    {#each list().items as product}\n      \u003cdiv class={styles.Item} data-variant=\"outline\"\u003e\n        \u003cdiv class={styles.ItemMedia}\u003e\n          \u003cimg src={product.image} alt={product.title} /\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003cdiv class={styles.ItemContent}\u003e\n          \u003cdiv  {/each}\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Dependencies\n\nAutomatically reload data when dependencies change, such as filter selections or external state.\n\n**Example: async-list/dependencies**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { useAsyncList } from '@ark-ui/react/collection'\nimport { LoaderIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/async-list.module.css'\n\nconst LIMIT = 5\n\ninterface User {\n  id: number\n  name: string\n  email: string\n  department: string\n  role: filterText }) {\n      await delay(400)\n\n      let items = mockUsers\n\n      if (selectedDepartment) {\n        items = items.filter((user) =\u003e user.department === selectedDepartment)\n          user.name.toLowerCase().includes(filterText.toLowerCase()) ||\n            user.email.toLowerCase().includes(filterText.toLowerCase()),\n        )\n      }\n\n      return { items: \u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/div\u003e\n        ))}\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      {list.items.length === 0 \u0026\u0026 !list.loading \u0026\u0026 (\n Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { useAsyncList } from '@ark-ui/solid/collection'\nimport { LoaderIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { createSignal, For } from 'solid-js'\nimport field from =\u003e Promise\u003cLoadResult\u003cT, C\u003e\u003e`) - Function to load data asynchronously\n- **sort** (`(params: SortParams\u003cT\u003e) =\u003e Promise\u003cSortResult\u003cT\u003e\u003e | SortResult\u003cT\u003e`) - Optional function for client-side\n  sorting\n- **autoReload** (`boolean`, default: `false`) - Whether to automatically reload data on mount\n- **initialItems** (`T[]`, default: `[]`) - Initial items to display before first load\n- **dependencies** (`any[]`, default: `[]`) - Values that trigger a reload when changed\n- **initialFilterText** (`string`, default: `''`) - Initial filter text value\n- **initialSortDescriptor** (`SortDescriptor | null`) - Initial sort configuration\n\n### Load Parameters\n\nThe `load` function receives an object with the following properties:\n\n- **cursor** (`C | undefined`) - Current cursor for pagination\n- **filterText** (`string`) - Current filter text\n- **sortDescriptor** (`SortDescriptor | null`) - Current sort configuration\n- **signal** (`AbortSignal`) - AbortController signal for request cancellation\n\n### Load Result\n\nThe `load` function should return an object with:\n\n- **items** (`T[]`) - The loaded items\n- **cursor** (`C | undefined`) - Optional cursor for next page\n\n### Sort Parameters\n\nThe `sort` function receives an object with:\n\n- **items** (`T[]`) - Current items to sort\n- **descriptor** (`SortDescriptor`) - Sort configuration with `column` and `direction`\n\n### Return Value\n\nThe hook returns an object with the following properties and methods:\n\n#### State Properties\n\n- **items** (`T[]`) - Current list of items\n- **loading** (`boolean`) - Whether a load operation is in progress\n- **error** (`Error | null`) - Any error from the last operation\n- **cursor** (`C | undefined`) - Current cursor for pagination\n- **filterText** (`string`) - Current filter text\n- **sortDescriptor** (`SortDescriptor | null`) - Current sort configuration\n\n#### Methods\n\n- **reload** (`() =\u003e void`) - Reload data from the beginning\n- **loadMore** (`() =\u003e void`) - Load more items (when cursor is available)\n- **setFilterText** (`(text: string) =\u003e void`) - Set filter text and reload\n- **sort** (`(descriptor: SortDescriptor) =\u003e void`) - Apply sorting\n\n#### Types\n\n```tsx\ninterface SortDescriptor {\n  column: string\n  direction: 'ascending' | 'descending'\n}\n\ninterface LoadParams\u003cC\u003e {\n  cursor?: C\n  filterText: string\n  sortDescriptor?: SortDescriptor | null\n  signal: AbortSignal\n}\n\ninterface LoadResult\u003cT, C\u003e {\n  items: T[]\n  cursor?: C\n}\n```"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"14:[\"$\",\"div\",null,{\"ref\":\"$undefined\",\"className\":\"pos_relative w_100% max-w_8xl
